[line truncated]\n2: \n3: HttpRouter is a lightweight high performance HTTP request router (also called *multiplexer* or just *mux* for short) for [Go](https://golang.org/).\n4: \n5: In contrast to the [default mux](https://golang.org/pkg/net/http/#ServeMux) of Go's `net/http` package, this router supports variables in the routing pattern and matches against the request method. It also scales better.\n6: \n7: The router is optimized for high performance and a small memory footprint. It scales well even with very long paths and a large number of routes. A compressing dynamic trie (radix tree) structure is used for efficient matching.\n8: \n9: ","endLine":9,"startLine":1}],"file":"vendor/github.com/julienschmidt/httprouter/README.md","repo":"github.com/sg-evals/grafana-mimir","type":"file","url":"https://sourcegraph.sourcegraph.com/github.com/sg-evals/grafana-mimir/-/blob/vendor/github.com/julienschmidt/httprouter/README.md"},{"chunks":[{"content":"246: \n247: func handleHTTPGRPCRequestWithOTel(ctx context.Context, req any, httpRequest *http.Request, router *mux.Router, handler grpc.UnaryHandler) (any, error) {\n248: \t// extract relevant span & tag data from request\n249: \tmethod := httpRequest.Method\n250: \trouteName := getRouteName(router, httpRequest)\n251: \turlPath := httpRequest.URL.Path\n252: \tuserAgent := httpRequest.Header.Get(\"User-Agent\")\n253: \n254: ","endLine":254,"startLine":246},{"content":"202: \n203: func handleHTTPGRPCRequestWithOpenTracing(ctx context.Context, req any, httpRequest *http.Request, router *mux.Router, handler grpc.UnaryHandler) (any, error) {\n204: \ttracer := opentracing.GlobalTracer()\n205: ","endLine":205,"startLine":202},{"content":"198: \n199: \t\treturn handleHTTPGRPCRequestWithOTel(ctx, req, httpRequest, router, handler)\n200: \t}\n201: ","endLine":201,"startLine":198}],"file":"vendor/github.com/grafana/dskit/middleware/http_tracing.go","repo":"github.com/sg-evals/grafana-mimir","type":"file","url":"https://sourcegraph.sourcegraph.com/github.com/sg-evals/grafana-mimir/-/blob/vendor/github.com/grafana/dskit/middleware/http_tracing.go"}]}}}

Required for the rules API\n98: \ts.HTTP.UseEncodedPath()\n99: \n100: \tvar sourceIPs *middleware.SourceIPExtractor\n101: \tif serverCfg.LogSourceIPs {\n102: \t\tvar err error\n103: \t\tsourceIPs, err = middleware.NewSourceIPs(serverCfg.LogSourceIPsHeader, serverCfg.LogSourceIPsRegex, serverCfg.LogSourceIPsFull)\n104: \t\tif err != nil {\n105: \t\t\t// This should have already been caught in the Server creation\n106: \t\t\treturn nil, err\n107: \t\t}\n108: \t}\n109: \n110: \tapi := &API{\n111: \t\tcfg:            cfg,\n112: \t\tAuthMiddleware: cfg.HTTPAuthMiddleware,\n113: \t\tserver:         s,\n114: \t\tlogger:         logger,\n115: \t\tsourceIPs:      sourceIPs,\n116: \t\tindexPage:      newIndexPageContent(),\n117: \t}\n118: \n119: \t// If no authentication middleware is present in the config, use the default authentication middleware.\n120: \tif api.AuthMiddleware == nil {\n121: \t\tapi.AuthMiddleware = middleware.AuthenticateUser\n122: \t}\n123: \n124: \t// Unconditionally add middleware that ensures we only accept requests with an expected number of tenants\n125: \t// that is applied after any existing auth middleware has run. methods ...string) {\n153: \tmethods = append([]string{method}, methods...)\n154: \tlevel.Debug(a.logger).Log(\"msg\", \"api: registering route\", \"methods\", strings.Join(methods, \",\"), \"path\", a.server.HTTP.Path(path)\n178: \t}\n179: \tif len(methods) > 0 {\n180: \t\troute = route.Methods(methods...)\n181: \t}\n182: \troute = route.Handler(handler)\n183: \n184: \treturn route\n185: }\n186: := time.Time{}\n427: \n428: \t\tlevel.Debug(a.logger).Log(\"msg\", \"disabling HTTP server timeouts for URL\", \"url\", r.URL)\n429: \n430: \t\tif err := c.SetReadDeadline(zero); err != nil {\n431:
